  6. Yāya āpattiyā saṃghena, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kataṃ hoti sā āpatti na āpajjitabbā, He should not commit the same offense as the offense for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense.
  7. aññā vā tādisikā, He should not commit an offense similar to the offense for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense.
  8. tato vā pāpiṭṭhatarā; He should not commit an offense worse than the offense for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense.
  9. kammaṃ na garahitabbaṃ, He should not criticize the procedure.
  10. kammikā na garahitabbā. He should not criticize those who did the procedure.
  11. Na pakatattassa bhikkhuno abhivādanaṃ, He should not consent to a regular monk bowing down to him.
  12. paccuṭṭhānaṃ, He should not consent to a regular monk standing up for him.
  13. añjalikammaṃ, He should not consent to a regular monk putting the palms of his hands together for him.
  14. sāmīcikammaṃ, He should not consent to a regular monk doing appropriate duties for him.
  15. āsanābhihāro, He should not consent to a regular monk offering him a seat.
  16. seyyābhihāro, He should not consent to a regular monk offering him a bed.
  17. pādodakaṃ pādapīṭhaṃ, He should not consent to a regular monk offering him water for washing his feet and a foot-stool.
  18. pādakathalikaṃ, He should not consent to a regular monk offering him a foot-scraper.
  19. pattacīvarappaṭiggahaṇaṃ, He should not consent to a regular monk receiving his bowl and robe.
  20. nahāne piṭṭhiparikammaṃ sāditabbaṃ. He should not consent to a regular monk massaging his back when bathing.
  21. Na pakatatto bhikkhu sīlavipattiyā anuddhaṃsetabbo, He should not accuse a regular monk of failure in morality.
  22. na ācāravipattiyā anuddhaṃsetabbo, He should not accuse a regular monk of failure in conduct.
  23. na diṭṭhivipattiyā anuddhaṃsetabbo, He should not accuse a regular monk of failure in view.
  24. na ājīvavipattiyā anuddhaṃsetabbo, He should not accuse a regular monk of failure in livelihood.
  25. na bhikkhu bhikkhūhi bhedetabbo. He should not cause splits between monks.
  26. Na gihiddhajo dhāretabbo, He should not wear lay clothes.
  27. na titthiyaddhajo dhāretabbo, He should not wear the robes of ascetics of other sects.
  28. na titthiyā sevitabbā; He should not associate with ascetics of other sects.
  29. bhikkhū sevitabbā, He should associate with monks.
  30. bhikkhusikkhāya sikkhitabbaṃ. He should train in the monks’ training.
  31. Na pakatattena bhikkhunā saddhiṃ ekacchanne āvāse vatthabbaṃ, He should not stay in the same room in a monastery as a regular monk.
  32. na ekacchanne anāvāse vatthabbaṃ, He should not stay in the same room in a non-monastery as a regular monk.
  33. na ekacchanne āvāse vā anāvāse vā vatthabbaṃ, He should not stay in the same room in a monastery or a non-monastery as a regular monk.
  34. pakatattaṃ bhikkhuṃ disvā āsanā vuṭṭhātabbaṃ, He should get up from his seat when he sees a regular monk.
  35. na pakatatto bhikkhu āsādetabbo anto vā bahi vā. He should not dismiss a regular monk, whether inside or outside a dwelling.
  36. Na pakatattassa bhikkhuno uposatho ṭhapetabbo, He should not cancel the observance-day ceremony of a regular monk.
  37. na pavāraṇā ṭhapetabbā, He should not cancel the invitation ceremony of a regular monk.
  38. na savacanīyaṃ kātabbaṃ, He should not speak to a regular monk to have him corrected or penalized.
  39. na anuvādo paṭṭhapetabbo, He should not criticize a regular monk.
  40. na okāso kāretabbo, He should not ask a regular monk for permission to accuse him of an offense.
  41. na codetabbo, He should not accuse a regular monk of an offense.
  42. na sāretabbo, He should not remind a regular monk of an offense.
  43. na bhikkhūhi sampayojetabban”ti. He should not associate inappropriately with other monks.”

Āpattiyā appaṭikamme ukkhepanīyakamme tecattālīsavattaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ. The forty-three kinds of conduct in regard to a legal procedure of ejection for not making amends for an offense are finished.

Atha kho saṃgho channassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ akāsi— Soon afterwards the Order did a legal procedure of ejecting the monk Channa for not making amends for an offense, asambhogaṃ saṃghena. prohibiting him from living with the Order. So saṃghena, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammakato tamhā āvāsā aññaṃ āvāsaṃ agamāsi. He then left that monastery and went to another one. Tattha bhikkhū neva abhivādesuṃ, na paccuṭṭhesuṃ, na añjalikammaṃ na sāmīcikammaṃ akaṃsu, na sakkariṃsu, na garuṃ kariṃsu, na mānesuṃ, na pūjesuṃ. The monks there did not bow down to him, stand up for him, put the palms of their hands together for him, or do appropriate duties for him. So bhikkhūhi asakkariyamāno agarukariyamāno amāniyamāno apūjiyamāno asakkārapakato tamhāpi āvāsā aññaṃ āvāsaṃ agamāsi. They did not honor, respect, and esteem him. Because of this, he left that monastery too and went to yet another one. Tatthapi bhikkhū neva abhivādesuṃ, na paccuṭṭhesuṃ, na añjalikammaṃ na sāmīcikammaṃ akaṃsu, na sakkariṃsu, na garuṃ kariṃsu, na mānesuṃ, na pūjesuṃ. There too the monks did not bow down to him, stand up for him, put the palms of their hands together for him, or do appropriate duties for him. So bhikkhūhi asakkariyamāno agarukariyamāno amāniyamāno apūjiyamāno asakkārapakato tamhāpi āvāsā aññaṃ āvāsaṃ agamāsi. They did not honor, respect, and esteem him. Because of this, he left that monastery too and went to yet another one. Tatthapi bhikkhū neva abhivādesuṃ, na paccuṭṭhesuṃ, na añjalikammaṃ na sāmīcikammaṃ akaṃsu, na sakkariṃsu, na garuṃ kariṃsu, na mānesuṃ, na pūjesuṃ. There too the monks did not bow down to him, stand up for him, put the palms of their hands together for him, or do appropriate duties for him. So bhikkhūhi asakkariyamāno agarukariyamāno amāniyamāno apūjiyamāno asakkārapakato punadeva kosambiṃ paccāgañchi. They did not honor, respect, and esteem him. Because of this, he left that monastery too and returned to Kosambī.

So sammā vattati, lomaṃ pāteti, netthāraṃ vattati, bhikkhū upasaṅkamitvā evaṃ vadeti— He then conducted himself properly and suitably so as to deserve to be released. He went to the monks “ahaṃ, āvuso, saṃghena, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammakato sammā vattāmi, lomaṃ pātemi, netthāraṃ vattāmi. and told them about this, Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? adding, “What should I do now?” Bhikkhū bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ … pe …. The monks told the Master … and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho channassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetu. “Well then, lift that procedure of ejecting the monk Channa for not making amends for an offense.”

6.5. Nappaṭippassambhetabbatecattālīsaka The group of forty-three on not to be lifted

Pañcahi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ nappaṭippassambhetabbaṃ. “When a monk has five qualities, a legal procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense should not be lifted: Upasampādeti, nissayaṃ deti, sāmaṇeraṃ upaṭṭhāpeti, bhikkhunovādakasammutiṃ sādiyati, sammatopi bhikkhuniyo ovadati— he gives the full ordination; he gives support; he has a novice monk attend on him; he accepts being appointed as an instructor of the nuns; he instructs the nuns, whether appointed or not. imehi kho, bhikkhave, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ nappaṭippassambhetabbaṃ.

Aparehipi, bhikkhave, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ nappaṭippassambhetabbaṃ. When a monk has another five qualities, a procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense should not be lifted: Yāya āpattiyā saṃghena, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kataṃ hoti taṃ āpattiṃ āpajjati, aññaṃ vā tādisikaṃ, tato vā pāpiṭṭhataraṃ; he commits the same offense for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense; he commits an offense similar to the one for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense; he commits an offense worse than the one for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense; kammaṃ garahati, kammike garahati … pe … he criticizes the procedure; he criticizes those who did the procedure. … pakatattassa bhikkhuno abhivādanaṃ, paccuṭṭhānaṃ, añjalikammaṃ, sāmīcikammaṃ, āsanābhihāraṃ sādiyati … pe … he consents to a regular monk bowing down to him; he consents to a regular monk standing up for him; he consents to a regular monk putting the palms of his hands together for him; he consents to a regular monk doing appropriate duties for him; he consents to a regular monk offering him a seat. … pakatattassa bhikkhuno seyyābhihāraṃ, pādodakaṃ pādapīṭhaṃ, pādakathalikaṃ, pattacīvarappaṭiggahaṇaṃ, nahāne piṭṭhiparikammaṃ sādiyati … pe … he consents to a regular monk offering him a bed; he consents to a regular monk offering him water for washing his feet and a foot-stool; he consents to a regular monk offering him a foot-scraper; he consents to a regular monk receiving his bowl and robe; he consents to a regular monk massaging his back when bathing. … pakatattaṃ bhikkhuṃ sīlavipattiyā anuddhaṃseti, ācāravipattiyā anuddhaṃseti, diṭṭhivipattiyā anuddhaṃseti, ājīvavipattiyā anuddhaṃseti, bhikkhuṃ bhikkhūhi bhedeti … pe … he accuses a regular monk of failure in morality; he accuses a regular monk of failure in conduct; he accuse a regular monk of failure in view; he accuses a regular monk of failure in livelihood; he causes splits between monks. … gihiddhajaṃ dhāreti, titthiyaddhajaṃ dhāreti, titthiye sevati, bhikkhū na sevati, bhikkhusikkhāya na sikkhati … pe … he wears lay clothes; he wears the robes of ascetics of other sects; he associates with ascetics of other sects; he does not associate with monks; he does not train in the monks’ training. … pakatattena bhikkhunā saddhiṃ ekacchanne āvāse vasati, ekacchanne anāvāse vasati, ekacchanne āvāse vā anāvāse vā vasati, pakatattaṃ bhikkhuṃ disvā āsanā na vuṭṭhāti, pakatattaṃ bhikkhuṃ āsādeti anto vā bahi vā— he stays in the same room in a monastery as a regular monk; he stays in the same room in a non-monastery as a regular monk; he stays in the same room in a monastery or a non-monastery as a regular monk; he does not get up from his seat when he sees a regular monk; he dismisses a regular monk, whether inside or outside a dwelling. imehi kho, bhikkhave, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ nappaṭippassambhetabbaṃ.

Aṭṭhahi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ nappaṭippassambhetabbaṃ. When a monk has eight qualities, a procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense should not be lifted: Pakatattassa bhikkhuno uposathaṃ ṭhapeti, pavāraṇaṃ ṭhapeti, savacanīyaṃ karoti, anuvādaṃ paṭṭhapeti, okāsaṃ kāreti, codeti, sāreti, bhikkhūhi sampayojeti— he cancels the observance-day ceremony of a regular monk; he cancels the invitation ceremony of a regular monk; he speaks to a regular monk to have him corrected or penalized; he criticizes a regular monk; he asks a regular monk for permission to accuse him of an offense; he accuses a regular monk of an offense; he reminds a regular monk of an offense; he associates inappropriately with other monks.” imehi kho, bhikkhave, aṭṭhahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ nappaṭippassambhetabbaṃ.

Āpattiyā appaṭikamme ukkhepanīyakamme nappaṭippassambhetabbatecattālīsakaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ. The group of forty-three on not to be lifted in regard to a legal procedure of ejection for not making amends for an offense is finished.

6.6. Paṭippassambhetabbatecattālīsaka The group of forty-three on to be lifted

Pañcahi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetabbaṃ. “When a monk has five qualities, a legal procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense should be lifted: Na upasampādeti, na nissayaṃ deti, na sāmaṇeraṃ upaṭṭhāpeti, na bhikkhunovādakasammutiṃ sādiyati, sammatopi bhikkhuniyo na ovadati— he does not give the full ordination; he does not give support; he does not have a novice monk attend on him; he does not accept being appointed as an instructor of the nuns; he does not instruct the nuns, whether appointed or not. imehi kho, bhikkhave, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetabbaṃ.

Aparehipi, bhikkhave, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetabbaṃ. When a monk has another five qualities, a procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense should be lifted: Yāya āpattiyā saṃghena, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kataṃ hoti taṃ āpattiṃ na āpajjati, aññaṃ vā tādisikaṃ, tato vā pāpiṭṭhataraṃ; he does not commit the same offense for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense; he does not commit an offense similar to the one for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense; he does not commit an offense worse than the one for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense; kammaṃ na garahati, kammike na garahati … pe … he does not criticize the procedure; he does not criticize those who did the procedure. … na pakatattassa bhikkhuno abhivādanaṃ, paccuṭṭhānaṃ, añjalikammaṃ, sāmīcikammaṃ, āsanābhihāraṃ sādiyati … pe … he does not consent to a regular monk bowing down to him; he does not consent to a regular monk standing up for him; he does not consent to a regular monk putting the palms of his hands together for him; he does not consent to a regular monk doing appropriate duties for him; he does not consent to a regular monk offering him a seat. … na pakatattassa bhikkhuno seyyābhihāraṃ, pādodakaṃ pādapīṭhaṃ, pādakathalikaṃ, pattacīvarappaṭiggahaṇaṃ, nahāne piṭṭhiparikammaṃ sādiyati … pe … he does not consent to a regular monk offering him a bed; he does not consent to a regular monk offering him water for washing his feet and a foot-stool; he does not consent to a regular monk offering him a foot-scraper; he does not consent to a regular monk receiving his bowl and robe; he does not consent to a regular monk massaging his back when bathing. … na pakatattaṃ bhikkhuṃ sīlavipattiyā anuddhaṃseti, na ācāravipattiyā anuddhaṃseti, na diṭṭhivipattiyā anuddhaṃseti, na ājīvavipattiyā anuddhaṃseti, na bhikkhuṃ bhikkhūhi bhedeti … pe … he does not accuse a regular monk of failure in morality; he does not accuse a regular monk of failure in conduct; he does not accuse a regular monk of failure in view; he does not accuse a regular monk of failure in livelihood; he does not cause splits between monks. … na gihiddhajaṃ dhāreti, na titthiyaddhajaṃ dhāreti, na titthiye sevati, bhikkhū sevati, bhikkhusikkhāya sikkhati … pe … he does not wear lay clothes; he does not wear the robes of ascetics of other sects; he does not associate with ascetics of other sects; he associates with monks; he trains in the monks’ training. … na pakatattena bhikkhunā saddhiṃ ekacchanne āvāse vasati, na ekacchanne anāvāse vasati, na ekacchanne āvāse vā anāvāse vā vasati, pakatattaṃ bhikkhuṃ disvā āsanā vuṭṭhāti, na pakatattaṃ bhikkhuṃ āsādeti anto vā bahi vā— he does not stay in the same room in a monastery as a regular monk; he does not stay in the same room in a non-monastery as a regular monk; he does not stay in the same room in a monastery or a non-monastery as a regular monk; he gets up from his seat when he sees a regular monk; he does not dismiss a regular monk, whether inside or outside a dwelling. imehi kho, bhikkhave, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetabbaṃ.

Aṭṭhahi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetabbaṃ. When a monk has eight qualities, a procedure of ejecting him for not making amends for an offense should be lifted: Na pakatattassa bhikkhuno uposathaṃ ṭhapeti, na pavāraṇaṃ ṭhapeti, na savacanīyaṃ karoti, na anuvādaṃ paṭṭhapeti, na okāsaṃ kāreti, na codeti, na sāreti, na bhikkhūhi sampayojeti— he does not cancel the observance-day ceremony of a regular monk; he does not cancel the invitation ceremony of a regular monk; he does not speak to a regular monk to have him corrected or penalized; he does not criticize a regular monk; he does not ask a regular monk for permission to accuse him of an offense; he does not accuse a regular monk of an offense; he does not remind a regular monk of an offense; he does not associate inappropriately with other monks.” imehi kho, bhikkhave, aṭṭhahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetabbaṃ.

Āpattiyā appaṭikamme ukkhepanīyakamme paṭippassambhetabbatecattālīsakaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ. The group of forty-three on to be lifted in regard to a legal procedure of ejection for not making amends for an offense is finished.

Evañca pana, bhikkhave, paṭippassambhetabbaṃ. “And this is how it should be lifted. Tena bhikkhave, channena bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā añjaliṃ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo— The monk Channa should approach the Order, put his upper robes over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, and say, ‘ahaṃ, bhante, saṃghena āpattiyā appaṭikamme ukkhepanīyakammakato sammā vattāmi, lomaṃ pātemi, netthāraṃ vattāmi, āpattiyā appaṭikamme ukkhepanīyassa kammassa paṭippassaddhiṃ yācāmī’ti. ‘Venerables, the Order has done a legal procedure of ejecting me for not making amends for an offense, but I have conducted myself properly and suitably so as to deserve to be released. I ask for the procedure of ejection to be lifted.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbā. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbā. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ channo bhikkhu saṃghena, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammakato sammā vattati, lomaṃ pāteti, netthāraṃ vattati, āpattiyā appaṭikamme ukkhepanīyassa kammassa paṭippassaddhiṃ yācati. The Order has done a legal procedure of ejecting the monk Channa for not making amends for an offense. He has conducted himself properly and suitably so as to deserve to be released, and now asks for the procedure of ejection to be lifted. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho channassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambheyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should lift the procedure of ejecting him. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ channo bhikkhu saṃghena, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammakato sammā vattati, lomaṃ pāteti, netthāraṃ vattati, āpattiyā appaṭikamme ukkhepanīyassa kammassa paṭippassaddhiṃ yācati. The Order has done a legal procedure of ejecting the monk Channa for not making amends for an offense. He has conducted himself properly and suitably so as to deserve to be released, and now asks for the procedure of ejection to be lifted. Saṃgho channassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambheti. Yassāyasmato khamati channassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyassa kammassa paṭippassaddhi, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of lifting the procedure of ejecting the monk Channa should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi— For the third time I speak on this matter. suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ channo bhikkhu saṃghena, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammakato sammā vattati, lomaṃ pāteti, netthāraṃ vattati, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyassa kammassa paṭippassaddhiṃ yācati. The Order has done a legal procedure of ejecting the monk Channa for not making amends for an offense. He has conducted himself properly and suitably so as to deserve to be released, and now asks for the procedure of ejection to be lifted. Saṃgho channassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambheti. Yassāyasmato khamati channassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyassa kammassa paṭippassaddhi, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of lifting the procedure of ejecting the monk Channa should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Paṭippassaddhaṃ saṃghena channassa bhikkhuno, āpattiyā appaṭikamme, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ. The Order has lifted the legal procedure of ejecting the monk Channa for not making amends for an offense. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

Āpattiyā appaṭikamme ukkhepanīyakammaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ. The sixth section on the legal procedure of ejection for not making amends for an offense is finished.

7. Pāpikāyadiṭṭhiyāappaṭinissagge ukkhepanīyakamma The legal procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view

Tena samayena buddho bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. At one time the Buddha was staying at Sāvatthī in the Jeta Grove, Anāthapiṇḍika’s Monastery. Tena kho pana samayena ariṭṭhassa nāma bhikkhuno gaddhabādhipubbassa evarūpaṃ pāpakaṃ diṭṭhigataṃ uppannaṃ hoti— At that time the monk Ariṭṭha, the ex-vulture-killer, had taken the following bad and erroneous view: “tathāhaṃ bhagavatā dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāmi yathā yeme antarāyikā dhammā vuttā bhagavatā te paṭisevato nālaṃ antarāyāyā”ti. “As I understand the Teaching of the Master, the things he calls obstructive are not able to obstruct one who indulges in them.”

Assosuṃ kho sambahulā bhikkhū ariṭṭhassa nāma kira bhikkhuno gaddhabādhipubbassa evarūpaṃ pāpakaṃ diṭṭhigataṃ uppannaṃ— A number of monks heard that Ariṭṭha had taken that view. “Tathāhaṃ bhagavatā dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāmi yathā yeme antarāyikā dhammā vuttā bhagavatā te paṭisevato nālaṃ antarāyāyā”ti.

Atha kho te bhikkhū yena ariṭṭho bhikkhu gaddhabādhipubbo tenupasaṅkamiṃsu. They went to him Upasaṅkamitvā ariṭṭhaṃ bhikkhuṃ gaddhabādhipubbaṃ etadavocuṃ— and asked, “saccaṃ kira te, āvuso ariṭṭha, evarūpaṃ pāpakaṃ diṭṭhigataṃ uppannaṃ— “Is it true, Ariṭṭha, that you have taken such a view?” tathāhaṃ bhagavatā dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāmi yathā yeme antarāyikā dhammā vuttā bhagavatā te paṭisevato nālaṃ antarāyāyā”ti?

“Evaṃ byā kho ahaṃ, āvuso, bhagavatā dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāmi, yathā yeme antarāyikā dhammā vuttā bhagavatā te paṭisevato nālaṃ antarāyāyā”ti. “Yes, indeed. As I understand the Master’s Teaching, the things he calls obstructive are not able to obstruct one who indulges in them.”

“Māvuso ariṭṭha, evaṃ avaca. “No, Ariṭṭha, Mā bhagavantaṃ abbhācikkhi. don’t misrepresent the Master, Na hi sādhu bhagavato abbhakkhānaṃ. for it’s not good to misrepresent him. Na hi bhagavā evaṃ vadeyya. The Master would never say such a thing. Anekapariyāyenāvuso ariṭṭha, antarāyikā dhammā antarāyikā vuttā bhagavatā. The Master has given many discourses about the obstructive things being obstructive Alañca pana te paṭisevato antarāyāya. and how they obstruct one who indulges in them. Appassādā kāmā vuttā bhagavatā, bahudukkhā bahupāyāsā, ādīnavo ettha bhiyyo. The Master has said that there is little enjoyment in sensual objects, but much suffering and much trouble, and that the danger in them is greater. Aṭṭhikaṅkalūpamā kāmā vuttā bhagavatā, bahudukkhā bahupāyāsā, ādīnavo ettha bhiyyo. The Master has said that sensual objects are similar to a skeleton … Maṃsapesūpamā kāmā vuttā bhagavatā … pe … similar to a piece of meat … tiṇukkūpamā kāmā vuttā bhagavatā … pe … similar to a grass torch … aṅgārakāsūpamā kāmā vuttā bhagavatā … similar to a pit of coals … supinakūpamā kāmā vuttā bhagavatā … similar to a dream … yācitakūpamā kāmā vuttā bhagavatā … similar to borrowed goods … rukkhaphalūpamā kāmā vuttā bhagavatā … similar to fruits on a tree … asisūnūpamā kāmā vuttā bhagavatā … similar to a knife and chopping block … sattisūlūpamā kāmā vuttā bhagavatā … similar to swords and stakes … sappasirūpamā kāmā vuttā bhagavatā, bahudukkhā bahupāyāsā, ādīnavo ettha bhiyyo”ti. similar to a snake’s head; they are much suffering and much trouble, and the danger in them is greater.”

Evampi kho ariṭṭho bhikkhu gaddhabādhipubbo tehi bhikkhūhi vuccamāno tatheva taṃ pāpakaṃ diṭṭhigataṃ thāmasā parāmāsā abhinivissa voharati— But even though the monks spoke to Ariṭṭha in this way, he stubbornly held on to that bad and erroneous view, and continued to insist on it. “evaṃ byā kho ahaṃ, āvuso, bhagavatā dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāmi, yathā yeme antarāyikā dhammā vuttā bhagavatā te paṭisevato nālaṃ antarāyāyā”ti. Yato ca kho te bhikkhū nāsakkhiṃsu ariṭṭhaṃ bhikkhuṃ gaddhabādhipubbaṃ etasmā pāpakā diṭṭhigatā vivecetuṃ, atha kho te bhikkhū yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu, upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. And since they were not able to make him give up that view, they approached the Master and told him what had happened.

Atha kho bhagavā etasmiṃ nidāne etasmiṃ pakaraṇe bhikkhusaṃghaṃ sannipātāpetvā ariṭṭhaṃ bhikkhuṃ gaddhabādhipubbaṃ paṭipucchi— The Master then had the Order of monks assembled and questioned Ariṭṭha:

“saccaṃ kira te, ariṭṭha, evarūpaṃ pāpakaṃ diṭṭhigataṃ uppannaṃ— “Is it true, Ariṭṭha, that you have taken a bad and erroneous view such as this: tathāhaṃ bhagavatā dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāmi yathā yeme antarāyikā dhammā vuttā bhagavatā te paṭisevato nālaṃ antarāyāyā”ti? ‘As I understand the Master’s Teaching, the things he calls obstructive are not able to obstruct one who indulges in them’?”

“Evaṃ byā kho ahaṃ, bhante, bhagavatā dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāmi, yathā yeme antarāyikā dhammā vuttā bhagavatā te paṭisevato nālaṃ antarāyāyā”ti. “Yes indeed, Venerable Sir.”

“Kassa nu kho nāma tvaṃ, moghapurisa, mayā evaṃ dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāsi? “Foolish man, who do you think I have taught in this way? Nanu mayā, moghapurisa, anekapariyāyena antarāyikā dhammā antarāyikā vuttā? Haven’t I given many discourses about the obstructive things being obstructive Alañca pana te paṭisevato antarāyāya. and how they obstruct one who indulges in them? Appassādā kāmā vuttā mayā, bahudukkhā bahupāyāsā, ādīnavo ettha bhiyyo. I have said that there is little enjoyment in sensual objects, but much suffering and much trouble, and that the danger in them is greater. Aṭṭhikaṅkalūpamā kāmā vuttā mayā, bahudukkhā bahupāyāsā, ādīnavo ettha bhiyyo. I have said that sensual objects are similar to a skeleton … Maṃsapesūpamā kāmā vuttā mayā … pe … similar to a piece of meat … tiṇukkūpamā kāmā vuttā mayā … similar to a grass torch … aṅgārakāsūpamā kāmā vuttā mayā … similar to a pit of coals … supinakūpamā kāmā vuttā mayā … similar to a dream … yācitakūpamā kāmā vuttā mayā … similar to borrowed goods … rukkhaphalūpamā kāmā vuttā mayā … similar to fruits on a tree … asisūnūpamā kāmā vuttā mayā … similar to a knife and chopping block … sattisūlūpamā kāmā vuttā mayā … similar to swords and stakes … sappasirūpamā kāmā vuttā mayā, bahudukkhā bahupāyāsā, ādīnavo ettha bhiyyo. similar to a snake’s head; they are much suffering and much trouble, and the danger in them is greater. Atha ca pana tvaṃ, moghapurisa, attanā duggahitena amhe ceva abbhācikkhasi, attānañca khaṇasi, bahuñca apuññaṃ pasavasi. And yet by misunderstanding, you have misrepresented me, hurt yourself, and made much demerit. Tañhi te, moghapurisa, bhavissati dīgharattaṃ ahitāya dukkhāya. This will be for your long-lasting harm and suffering. Netaṃ, moghapurisa, appasannānaṃ vā pasādāya … pe … This will not give rise to confidence in those without it …” … vigarahitvā … pe … and after rebuking him … dhammiṃ kathaṃ katvā bhikkhū āmantesi— he gave a teaching and addressed the monks:

“tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho ariṭṭhassa bhikkhuno gaddhabādhipubbassa, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ karotu— “Well then, the Order should do a procedure of ejecting Ariṭṭha for not giving up a bad view, asambhogaṃ saṃghena. prohibiting him from living with the Order. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, kātabbaṃ— And this is how it should be done. paṭhamaṃ ariṭṭho bhikkhu codetabbo, codetvā sāretabbo, sāretvā āpattiṃ āropetabbo, āpattiṃ āropetvā byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— First you should accuse the monk Ariṭṭha. He should then be reminded of what he has done, before he is charged with an offense. A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ariṭṭhassa bhikkhuno gaddhabādhipubbassa evarūpaṃ pāpakaṃ diṭṭhigataṃ uppannaṃ— This monk Ariṭṭha, the ex-vulture-killer, has taken the following bad and erroneous view: tathāhaṃ bhagavatā dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāmi yathā yeme antarāyikā dhammā vuttā bhagavatā te paṭisevato nālaṃ antarāyāyāti. “As I understand the Teaching of the Master, the things he calls obstructive are not able to obstruct one who indulges in them.” So taṃ diṭṭhiṃ na paṭinissajjati. He is not giving up that view. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho ariṭṭhassa bhikkhuno gaddhabādhipubbassa, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kareyya— If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should do a legal procedure of ejecting Ariṭṭha for not giving up a bad view, asambhogaṃ saṃghena. prohibiting him from living with the Order. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ariṭṭhassa bhikkhuno gaddhabādhipubbassa evarūpaṃ pāpakaṃ diṭṭhigataṃ uppannaṃ— This monk Ariṭṭha, the ex-vulture-killer, has taken the following bad and erroneous view: tathāhaṃ bhagavatā dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāmi yathā yeme antarāyikā dhammā vuttā bhagavatā te paṭisevato nālaṃ antarāyāyāti. “As I understand the Teaching of the Master, the things he calls obstructive are not able to obstruct one who indulges in them.” So taṃ diṭṭhiṃ na paṭinissajjati. He is not giving up that view. Saṃgho ariṭṭhassa bhikkhuno gaddhabādhipubbassa, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ karoti— The Order is doing a legal procedure of ejecting Ariṭṭha for not giving up a bad view, asambhogaṃ saṃghena. prohibiting him from living with the Order. Yassāyasmato khamati ariṭṭhassa bhikkhuno gaddhabādhipubbassa, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyassa kammassa karaṇaṃ— Any monk who approves of doing a procedure of ejecting Ariṭṭha for not giving up a bad view asambhogaṃ saṃghena, so tuṇhassa; should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi— For the third time I speak on this matter. suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ariṭṭhassa bhikkhuno gaddhabādhipubbassa evarūpaṃ pāpakaṃ diṭṭhigataṃ uppannaṃ— This monk Ariṭṭha, the ex-vulture-killer, has taken the following bad and erroneous view: tathāhaṃ bhagavatā dhammaṃ desitaṃ ājānāmi yathā yeme antarāyikā dhammā vuttā bhagavatā te paṭisevato nālaṃ antarāyāyāti. “As I understand the Teaching of the Master, the things he calls obstructive are not able to obstruct one who indulges in them.” So taṃ diṭṭhiṃ na paṭinissajjati. He is not giving up that view. Saṃgho ariṭṭhassa bhikkhuno gaddhabādhipubbassa, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ karoti— The Order is doing a legal procedure of ejecting Ariṭṭha for not giving up a bad view, asambhogaṃ saṃghena. prohibiting him from living with the Order. Yassāyasmato khamati ariṭṭhassa bhikkhuno gaddhabādhipubbassa, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyassa kammassa karaṇaṃ— Any monk who approves of doing a procedure of ejecting Ariṭṭha for not giving up a bad view asambhogaṃ saṃghena, so tuṇhassa; should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Kataṃ saṃghena ariṭṭhassa bhikkhuno gaddhabādhipubbassa, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ— The Order has done the legal procedure of ejecting Ariṭṭha for not giving up a bad view, asambhogaṃ saṃghena. prohibiting him from living with the Order. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’

Āvāsaparamparañca, bhikkhave, saṃsatha— Monks, you should proclaim from monastery to monastery ‘ariṭṭho bhikkhu gaddhabādhipubbo, saṃghena pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammakato— that the Order has done a legal procedure of ejecting Ariṭṭha for not giving up a bad view, asambhogaṃ saṃghenā’”ti. prohibiting him from living with the Order.”

7.1. Adhammakammadvādasaka The group of twelve on illegitimate legal procedures

“Tīhi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgataṃ, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ adhammakammañca hoti, avinayakammañca, duvūpasantañca. “When a legal procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has three qualities, it is illegitimate, not in accordance with the Monastic Law, and not properly disposed of: Asammukhā kataṃ hoti, appaṭipucchā kataṃ hoti, appaṭiññāya kataṃ hoti— it is done in the absence of the accused, it is done without questioning the accused, it is done without the admission of the accused. imehi kho, bhikkhave, tīhaṅgehi samannāgataṃ, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ adhammakammañca hoti, avinayakammañca, duvūpasantañca.

Aparehipi, bhikkhave, tīhaṅgehi samannāgataṃ, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ adhammakammañca hoti, avinayakammañca, duvūpasantañca. When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also illegitimate, not in accordance with the Monastic Law, and not properly disposed of: Anāpattiyā kataṃ hoti, adesanāgāminiyā āpattiyā kataṃ hoti, desitāya āpattiyā kataṃ hoti … pe … it is done against one who has not committed any offense, it is done against one who has committed an offense that is not clearable by confession, it is done against one who has confessed their offense.

acodetvā kataṃ hoti, asāretvā kataṃ hoti, āpattiṃ anāropetvā kataṃ hoti … pe … When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also illegitimate, not in accordance with the Monastic Law, and not properly disposed of: it is done without having accused the person of their offense, it is done without having reminded the person of their offense, it is done without having charged the person with their offense.

asammukhā kataṃ hoti, adhammena kataṃ hoti, vaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … “When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also illegitimate, not in accordance with the Monastic Law, and not properly disposed of: it is done in the absence of the accused, it is done illegitimately, it is done by an incomplete assembly.

appaṭipucchā kataṃ hoti, adhammena kataṃ hoti, vaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also illegitimate, not in accordance with the Monastic Law, and not properly disposed of: it is done without questioning the accused, it is done illegitimately, it is done by an incomplete assembly.

appaṭiññāya kataṃ hoti, adhammena kataṃ hoti, vaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also illegitimate, not in accordance with the Monastic Law, and not properly disposed of: it is done without the admission of the accused, it is done illegitimately, it is done by an incomplete assembly.

anāpattiyā kataṃ hoti, adhammena kataṃ hoti, vaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … “When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also illegitimate, not in accordance with the Monastic Law, and not properly disposed of: it is done against one who has not committed any offense, it is done illegitimately, it is done by an incomplete assembly.

adesanāgāminiyā āpattiyā kataṃ hoti, adhammena kataṃ hoti, vaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also illegitimate, not in accordance with the Monastic Law, and not properly disposed of: it is done against one who has committed an offense that is not clearable by confession, it is done illegitimately, it is done by an incomplete assembly.

desitāya āpattiyā kataṃ hoti, adhammena kataṃ hoti, vaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also illegitimate, not in accordance with the Monastic Law, and not properly disposed of: it is done against one who has confessed their offense, it is done illegitimately, it is done by an incomplete assembly.

acodetvā kataṃ hoti, adhammena kataṃ hoti, vaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … “When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also illegitimate, not in accordance with the Monastic Law, and not properly disposed of: it is done without having accused the person of their offense, it is done illegitimately, it is done by an incomplete assembly.

asāretvā kataṃ hoti, adhammena kataṃ hoti, vaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also illegitimate, not in accordance with the Monastic Law, and not properly disposed of: it is done without having reminded the person of their offense, it is done illegitimately, it is done by an incomplete assembly.

āpattiṃ anāropetvā kataṃ hoti, adhammena kataṃ hoti, vaggena kataṃ hoti— When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also illegitimate, not in accordance with the Monastic Law, and not properly disposed of: it is done without having charged the person with their offense, it is done illegitimately, it is done by an incomplete assembly.” imehi kho, bhikkhave, tīhaṅgehi samannāgataṃ, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ adhammakammañca hoti, avinayakammañca, duvūpasantañca.

Pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge ukkhepanīyakamme adhammakammadvādasakaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ. The group of twelve on illegitimate legal procedures of ejection for not giving up a bad view is finished.

7.2. Dhammakammadvādasaka The group of twelve on legitimate legal procedures

Tīhi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgataṃ, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ dhammakammañca hoti, vinayakammañca, suvūpasantañca. “When a legal procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has three qualities, it is legitimate, in accordance with the Monastic Law, and properly disposed of: Sammukhā kataṃ hoti, paṭipucchā kataṃ hoti, paṭiññāya kataṃ hoti— it is done in the presence of the accused, it is done with the questioning of the accused, it is done with the admission of the accused. imehi kho, bhikkhave, tīhaṅgehi samannāgataṃ, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ dhammakammañca hoti, vinayakammañca, suvūpasantañca.

Aparehipi, bhikkhave, tīhaṅgehi samannāgataṃ, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ dhammakammañca hoti, vinayakammañca, suvūpasantañca. When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also legitimate, in accordance with the Monastic Law, and properly disposed of: Āpattiyā kataṃ hoti, desanāgāminiyā āpattiyā kataṃ hoti, adesitāya āpattiyā kataṃ hoti … pe … it is done against one who has committed an offense, it is done against one who has committed an offense that is clearable by confession, it is done against one who has not confessed their offense.

codetvā kataṃ hoti, sāretvā kataṃ hoti, āpattiṃ āropetvā kataṃ hoti … pe … When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also legitimate, in accordance with the Monastic Law, and properly disposed of: it is done after having accused the person of their offense, it is done after having reminded the person of their offense, it is done after having charged the person with their offense.

sammukhā kataṃ hoti, dhammena kataṃ hoti, samaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … “When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also legitimate, in accordance with the Monastic Law, and properly disposed of: it is done in the presence of the accused, it is done legitimately, it is done by a complete assembly.

paṭipucchā kataṃ hoti, dhammena kataṃ hoti, samaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also legitimate, in accordance with the Monastic Law, and properly disposed of: it is done with the questioning of the accused, it is done legitimately, it is done by a complete assembly.

paṭiññāya kataṃ hoti, dhammena kataṃ hoti, samaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also legitimate, in accordance with the Monastic Law, and properly disposed of: it is done with the admission of the accused, it is done legitimately, it is done by a complete assembly.

āpattiyā kataṃ hoti, dhammena kataṃ hoti, samaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … “When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also legitimate, in accordance with the Monastic Law, and properly disposed of: it is done against one who has committed an offense, it is done legitimately, it is done by a complete assembly.

desanāgāminiyā āpattiyā kataṃ hoti, dhammena kataṃ hoti, samaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also legitimate, in accordance with the Monastic Law, and properly disposed of: it is done against one who has committed an offense that is clearable by confession, it is done legitimately, it is done by a complete assembly.

adesitāya āpattiyā kataṃ hoti, dhammena kataṃ hoti, samaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also legitimate, in accordance with the Monastic Law, and properly disposed of: it is done against one who has not confessed their offense, it is done legitimately, it is done by a complete assembly.

codetvā kataṃ hoti, dhammena kataṃ hoti, samaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … “When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also legitimate, in accordance with the Monastic Law, and properly disposed of: it is done after having accused the person of their offense, it is done legitimately, it is done by a complete assembly.

sāretvā kataṃ hoti, dhammena kataṃ hoti, samaggena kataṃ hoti … pe … When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also legitimate, in accordance with the Monastic Law, and properly disposed of: it is done after having reminded the person of their offense, it is done legitimately, it is done by a complete assembly.

āpattiṃ āropetvā kataṃ hoti, dhammena kataṃ hoti, samaggena kataṃ hoti— When a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view has another three qualities, it is also legitimate, in accordance with the Monastic Law, and properly disposed of: it is done after having charged the person with their offense, it is done legitimately, it is done by a complete assembly.” imehi kho, bhikkhave, tīhaṅgehi samannāgataṃ, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ dhammakammañca hoti, vinayakammañca, suvūpasantañca.

Pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge ukkhepanīyakamme dhammakammadvādasakaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ. The group of twelve on legitimate legal procedures of ejection for not giving up a bad view is finished.

7.3. Ākaṅkhamānachakka The group of six on wishing

Tīhi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, ākaṅkhamāno saṃgho, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kareyya. “When a monk has three qualities, the Order may, if it wishes, do a legal procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view: Bhaṇḍanakārako hoti kalahakārako vivādakārako bhassakārako saṃghe adhikaraṇakārako; he is quarrelsome, disputatious, and a creator of legal issues in the Order; bālo hoti abyatto āpattibahulo anapadāno; he is ignorant and incompetent, often committing offenses, incapable of determining whether he has committed an offense; gihisaṃsaṭṭho viharati ananulomikehi gihisaṃsaggehi— he is constantly and improperly socializing with lay people. imehi kho, bhikkhave, tīhaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, ākaṅkhamāno saṃgho, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kareyya. #1

Aparehipi, bhikkhave, tīhaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, ākaṅkhamāno saṃgho, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kareyya. When a monk has another three qualities, the Order may, if it wishes, do a procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view: Adhisīle sīlavipanno hoti, ajjhācāre ācāravipanno hoti, atidiṭṭhiyā diṭṭhivipanno hoti— he has failed in the higher morality; he has failed in the higher conduct; he has failed in view. imehi kho, bhikkhave, tīhaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, ākaṅkhamāno saṃgho, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kareyya. #2

Aparehipi, bhikkhave, tīhaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, ākaṅkhamāno saṃgho, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kareyya. When a monk has another three qualities, the Order may, if it wishes, do a procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view: Buddhassa avaṇṇaṃ bhāsati, dhammassa avaṇṇaṃ bhāsati, saṃghassa avaṇṇaṃ bhāsati— he disparages the Buddha; he disparages the Teaching; he disparages the Order. imehi kho, bhikkhave, tīhaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, ākaṅkhamāno saṃgho, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kareyya. #3

Tiṇṇaṃ, bhikkhave, bhikkhūnaṃ, ākaṅkhamāno saṃgho, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kareyya. “The Order may, if it wishes, do a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view against three kinds of monks: Eko bhaṇḍanakārako hoti kalahakārako vivādakārako bhassakārako saṃghe adhikaraṇakārako; those who are quarrelsome, disputatious, and creators of legal issues in the Order; eko bālo hoti abyatto āpattibahulo anapadāno; those who are ignorant and incompetent, often committing offenses, incapable of determining whether they have committed an offense; eko gihisaṃsaṭṭho viharati ananulomikehi gihisaṃsaggehi— those who are constantly and improperly socializing with lay people. imesaṃ kho, bhikkhave, tiṇṇaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ, ākaṅkhamāno saṃgho, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kareyya. #4

Aparesampi, bhikkhave, tiṇṇaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ, ākaṅkhamāno saṃgho, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kareyya. The Order may, if it wishes, do a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view against another three kinds of monks: Eko adhisīle sīlavipanno hoti, eko ajjhācāre ācāravipanno hoti, eko atidiṭṭhiyā diṭṭhivipanno hoti— those who have failed in the higher morality; those who have failed in the higher conduct; those who have failed in view. imesaṃ kho, bhikkhave, tiṇṇaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ, ākaṅkhamāno saṃgho, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kareyya. #5

Aparesampi, bhikkhave, tiṇṇaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ, ākaṅkhamāno saṃgho, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kareyya. The Order may, if it wishes, do a procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view against another three kinds of monks: Eko buddhassa avaṇṇaṃ bhāsati, eko dhammassa avaṇṇaṃ bhāsati, eko saṃghassa avaṇṇaṃ bhāsati— those who disparage the Buddha; those who disparage the Teaching; those who disparage the Order.” imesaṃ kho, bhikkhave, tiṇṇaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ, ākaṅkhamāno saṃgho, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissage, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kareyya. #6

Pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissage ukkhepanīyakamme ākaṅkhamānachakkaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ. The group of six on wishing in regard to a legal procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view is finished.

7.4. Tecattālīsavatta The forty-three kinds of conduct

Pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge ukkhepanīyakammakatena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā sammā vattitabbaṃ. “A monk who has had a legal procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view done against himself, should conduct himself properly. Tatrāyaṃ sammāvattanā— This is the proper conduct:

  1. na upasampādetabbaṃ, He should not give the full ordination.
  2. na nissayo dātabbo, He should not give support.
  3. na sāmaṇero upaṭṭhāpetabbo, He should not have a novice monk attend on him.
  4. na bhikkhunovādakasammuti sāditabbā, He should not accept being appointed as an instructor of the nuns.
  5. sammatenapi bhikkhuniyo na ovaditabbā. Even if appointed, he should not instruct the nuns.
  6. Yāya āpattiyā saṃghena, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kataṃ hoti sā āpatti na āpajjitabbā,
  7. aññā vā tādisikā,
  8. tato vā pāpiṭṭhatarā;
  9. kammaṃ na garahitabbaṃ, He should not criticize the procedure.
  10. kammikā na garahitabbā … pe …, He should not criticize those who did the procedure.
  11. He should not consent to a regular monk bowing down to him.
  12. He should not consent to a regular monk standing up for him.
  13. He should not consent to a regular monk putting the palms of his hands together for him.
  14. He should not consent to a regular monk doing appropriate duties for him.
  15. He should not consent to a regular monk offering him a seat.
  16. He should not consent to a regular monk offering him a bed.
  17. He should not consent to a regular monk offering him water for washing his feet and a foot-stool.
  18. He should not consent to a regular monk offering him a foot-scraper.
  19. He should not consent to a regular monk receiving his bowl and robe.
  20. He should not consent to a regular monk massaging his back when bathing.
  21. He should not accuse a regular monk of failure in morality.
  22. He should not accuse a regular monk of failure in conduct.
  23. He should not accuse a regular monk of failure in view.
  24. He should not accuse a regular monk of failure in livelihood.
  25. He should not cause splits between monks.
  26. He should not wear lay clothes.
  27. He should not wear the robes of ascetics of other sects.
  28. He should not associate with ascetics of other sects.
  29. He should associate with monks.
  30. He should train in the monks’ training.
  31. He should not stay in the same room in a monastery as a regular monk.
  32. He should not stay in the same room in a non-monastery as a regular monk.
  33. He should not stay in the same room in a monastery or a non-monastery as a regular monk.
  34. He should get up from his seat when he sees a regular monk.
  35. He should not dismiss a regular monk, whether inside or outside a dwelling.
  36. na pakatattassa bhikkhuno uposatho ṭhapetabbo, He should not cancel the observance-day ceremony of a regular monk.
  37. na pavāraṇā ṭhapetabbā, He should not cancel the invitation ceremony of a regular monk.
  38. na savacanīyaṃ kātabbaṃ, He should not speak to a regular monk to have him corrected or penalized.
  39. na anuvādo paṭṭhapetabbo, He should not criticize a regular monk.
  40. na okāso kāretabbo, He should not ask a regular monk for permission to accuse him of an offense.
  41. na codetabbo, He should not accuse a regular monk of an offense.
  42. na sāretabbo, He should not remind a regular monk of an offense.
  43. na bhikkhūhi sampayojetabban”ti. He should not associate inappropriately with other monks.”

Pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge ukkhepanīyakamme tecattālīsavattaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ. The forty-three kinds of conduct in regard to a legal procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view are finished.

Atha kho saṃgho ariṭṭhassa bhikkhuno gaddhabādhipubbassa, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ akāsi— Soon afterwards the Order did a legal procedure of ejecting Ariṭṭha for not giving up a bad view, asambhogaṃ saṃghena. prohibiting him from living with the Order. So saṃghena, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammakato vibbhami. He then disrobed. Ye te bhikkhū appicchā … pe … te ujjhāyanti khiyyanti vipācenti— The monks of few desires complained and criticized him, “kathañhi nāma ariṭṭho bhikkhu gaddhabādhipubbo saṃghena, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammakato vibbhamissatī”ti? “How could the monk Ariṭṭha disrobe after the Order had done a procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view?” Atha kho te bhikkhū bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. The monks told the Master.

Atha kho bhagavā etasmiṃ nidāne etasmiṃ pakaraṇe bhikkhusaṃghaṃ sannipātāpetvā bhikkhū paṭipucchi— Soon afterwards he had the Order of monks assembled and questioned them:

“saccaṃ kira, bhikkhave, ariṭṭho bhikkhu gaddhabādhipubbo saṃghena, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammakato vibbhamatī”ti? “Is it true, monks, that the monk Ariṭṭha disrobed after the Order had done a procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view?”

“Saccaṃ, bhagavā”ti. “It’s true, Master.”

Vigarahi buddho bhagavā— The Master criticized him … “ananucchavikaṃ … pe … “It’s not suitable … kathañhi nāma so, bhikkhave, moghapuriso saṃghena, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammakato vibbhamissati? How can that foolish man disrobe after the Order has done a procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view? Netaṃ, bhikkhave, appasannānaṃ vā pasādāya … pe … This will not give rise to confidence in those without it …” … vigarahitvā … pe … After criticizing him … dhammiṃ kathaṃ katvā bhikkhū āmantesi— he gave a teaching and addressed the monks:

“tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetu. “Well then, the Order should lift that procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view.”

7.5. Nappaṭippassambhetabbatecattālīsaka The group of forty-three on not to be lifted

Pañcahi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ nappaṭippassambhetabbaṃ. “When a monk has five qualities, a legal procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view should not be lifted: Upasampādeti, nissayaṃ deti, sāmaṇeraṃ upaṭṭhāpeti, bhikkhunovādakasammutiṃ sādiyati, sammatopi bhikkhuniyo ovadati— he gives the full ordination; he gives support; he has a novice monk attend on him; he accepts being appointed as an instructor of the nuns; he instructs the nuns, whether appointed or not. imehi kho, bhikkhave, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissage, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ nappaṭippassambhetabbaṃ.

Aparehipi, bhikkhave, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ nappaṭippassambhetabbaṃ. When a monk has another five qualities, a procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view should not be lifted: Yāya āpattiyā saṃghena pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kataṃ hoti taṃ āpattiṃ āpajjati, aññaṃ vā tādisikaṃ, tato vā pāpiṭṭhataraṃ; he commits the same offense for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view; he commits an offense similar to the one for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view; he commits an offense worse than the one for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view; kammaṃ garahati, kammike garahati— he criticizes the procedure; he criticizes those who did the procedure. … imehi kho, bhikkhave, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ nappaṭippassambhetabbaṃ … pe …. he consents to a regular monk bowing down to him; he consents to a regular monk standing up for him; he consents to a regular monk putting the palms of his hands together for him; he consents to a regular monk doing appropriate duties for him; he consents to a regular monk offering him a seat. … he consents to a regular monk offering him a bed; he consents to a regular monk offering him water for washing his feet and a foot-stool; he consents to a regular monk offering him a foot-scraper; he consents to a regular monk receiving his bowl and robe; he consents to a regular monk massaging his back when bathing. … he accuses a regular monk of failure in morality; he accuses a regular monk of failure in conduct; he accuse a regular monk of failure in view; he accuses a regular monk of failure in livelihood; he causes splits between monks. … he wears lay clothes; he wears the robes of ascetics of other sects; he associates with ascetics of other sects; he does not associate with monks; he does not train in the monks’ training. … he stays in the same room in a monastery as a regular monk; he stays in the same room in a non-monastery as a regular monk; he stays in the same room in a monastery or a non-monastery as a regular monk; he does not get up from his seat when he sees a regular monk; he dismisses a regular monk, whether inside or outside a dwelling.

Aṭṭhahi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ nappaṭippassambhetabbaṃ. When a monk has eight qualities, a procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view should not be lifted: Pakatattassa bhikkhuno uposathaṃ ṭhapeti, pavāraṇaṃ ṭhapeti, savacanīyaṃ karoti, anuvādaṃ paṭṭhapeti, okāsaṃ kāreti, codeti, sāreti, bhikkhūhi sampayojeti— he cancels the observance-day ceremony of a regular monk; he cancels the invitation ceremony of a regular monk; he speaks to a regular monk to have him corrected or penalized; he criticizes a regular monk; he asks a regular monk for permission to accuse him of an offense; he accuses a regular monk of an offense; he reminds a regular monk of an offense; he associates inappropriately with other monks.” imehi kho, bhikkhave, aṭṭhahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ nappaṭippassambhetabbaṃ.

Pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge ukkhepanīyakamme nappaṭippassambhetabbatecattālīsakaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ. The group of forty-three on not to be lifted in regard to a legal procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view is finished.

7.6. Paṭippassambhetabbatecattālīsaka The group of forty-three on to be lifted

Pañcahi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetabbaṃ. “When a monk has five qualities, a legal procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view should be lifted: Na upasampādeti, na nissayaṃ deti, na sāmaṇeraṃ upaṭṭhāpeti, na bhikkhunovādakasammutiṃ sādiyati, sammatopi bhikkhuniyo na ovadati— he does not give the full ordination; he does not give support; he does not have a novice monk attend on him; he does not accept being appointed as an instructor of the nuns; he does not instruct the nuns, whether appointed or not. imehi kho, bhikkhave, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetabbaṃ.

Aparehipi, bhikkhave, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetabbaṃ. When a monk has another five qualities, a procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view should be lifted: Yāya āpattiyā saṃghena, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ kataṃ hoti taṃ āpattiṃ na āpajjati, aññaṃ vā tādisikaṃ, tato vā pāpiṭṭhataraṃ; he does not commit the same offense for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view; he does not commit an offense similar to the one for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view; he does not commit an offense worse than the one for which the Order did the procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view; kammaṃ na garahati, kammike na garahati— he does not criticize the procedure; he does not criticize those who did the procedure. … imehi kho, bhikkhave, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetabbaṃ … pe …. he does not consent to a regular monk bowing down to him; he does not consent to a regular monk standing up for him; he does not consent to a regular monk putting the palms of his hands together for him; he does not consent to a regular monk doing appropriate duties for him; he does not consent to a regular monk offering him a seat. … he does not consent to a regular monk offering him a bed; he does not consent to a regular monk offering him water for washing his feet and a foot-stool; he does not consent to a regular monk offering him a foot-scraper; he does not consent to a regular monk receiving his bowl and robe; he does not consent to a regular monk massaging his back when bathing. … he does not accuse a regular monk of failure in morality; he does not accuse a regular monk of failure in conduct; he does not accuse a regular monk of failure in view; he does not accuse a regular monk of failure in livelihood; he does not cause splits between monks. … he does not wear lay clothes; he does not wear the robes of ascetics of other sects; he does not associate with ascetics of other sects; he associates with monks; he trains in the monks’ training. … he does not stay in the same room in a monastery as a regular monk; he does not stay in the same room in a non-monastery as a regular monk; he does not stay in the same room in a monastery or a non-monastery as a regular monk; he gets up from his seat when he sees a regular monk; he does not dismiss a regular monk, whether inside or outside a dwelling.

Aṭṭhahi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetabbaṃ. When a monk has eight qualities, a procedure of ejecting him for not giving up a bad view should be lifted: Na pakatattassa bhikkhuno uposathaṃ ṭhapeti, na pavāraṇaṃ ṭhapeti, na savacanīyaṃ karoti, na anuvādaṃ paṭṭhapeti, na okāsaṃ kāreti, na codeti, na sāreti, na bhikkhūhi sampayojeti— he does not cancel the observance-day ceremony of a regular monk; he does not cancel the invitation ceremony of a regular monk; he does not speak to a regular monk to have him corrected or penalized; he does not criticize a regular monk; he does not ask a regular monk for permission to accuse him of an offense; he does not accuse a regular monk of an offense; he does not remind a regular monk of an offense; he does not associate inappropriately with other monks.” imehi kho, bhikkhave, aṭṭhahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambhetabbaṃ.

Pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge ukkhepanīyakamme paṭippassambhetabbatecattālīsakaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ. The group of forty-three on to be lifted in regard to a legal procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view is finished.

Evañca pana, bhikkhave, paṭippassambhetabbaṃ. “And, monks, this is how it should be lifted. Tena, bhikkhave, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammakatena bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā añjaliṃ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo— The monk who has been ejected by the Order for not giving up a bad view should approach the Order, put his upper robes over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, and say, ‘ahaṃ, bhante, saṃghena, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammakato sammā vattāmi, lomaṃ pātemi, netthāraṃ vattāmi, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyassa kammassa paṭippassaddhiṃ yācāmī’ti. ‘Venerables, the Order has done a legal procedure of ejecting me for not giving up a bad view, but I have conducted myself properly and suitably so as to deserve to be released. I ask for the procedure of ejection to be lifted.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbā. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbā. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu saṃghena, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammakato sammā vattati, lomaṃ pāteti, netthāraṃ vattati, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyassa kammassa paṭippassaddhiṃ yācati. The Order has done a legal procedure of ejecting monk so-and-so for not giving up a bad view. He has conducted himself properly and suitably so as to deserve to be released, and now asks for the procedure of ejection to be lifted. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambheyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should lift the procedure of ejecting him. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu saṃghena, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammakato sammā vattati, lomaṃ pāteti, netthāraṃ vattati, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyassa kammassa paṭippassaddhiṃ yācati. The Order has done a legal procedure of ejecting monk so-and-so for not giving up a bad view. He has conducted himself properly and suitably so as to deserve to be released, and now asks for the procedure of ejection to be lifted. Saṃgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambheti. Yassāyasmato khamati itthannāmassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyassa kammassa paṭippassaddhi, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of lifting the procedure of ejecting monk so-and-so should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi— For the third time I speak on this matter. suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu saṃghena, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammakato sammā vattati, lomaṃ pāteti, netthāraṃ vattati, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge ukkhepanīyassa kammassa paṭippassaddhiṃ yācati. The Order has done a legal procedure of ejecting monk so-and-so for not giving up a bad view. He has conducted himself properly and suitably so as to deserve to be released, and now asks for the procedure of ejection to be lifted. Saṃgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ paṭippassambheti. Yassāyasmato khamati itthannāmassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyassa kammassa paṭippassaddhi, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of lifting the procedure of ejecting monk so-and-so should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Paṭippassaddhaṃ saṃghena itthannāmassa bhikkhuno, pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge, ukkhepanīyakammaṃ. The Order has lifted the legal procedure of ejecting monk so-and-so for not giving up a bad view. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

Pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge ukkhepanīyakammaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ sattamaṃ. The seventh section on the legal procedure of ejection for not giving up a bad view is finished.

Kammakkhandhako paṭhamo. Imamhi khandhake vatthū satta. The first chapter on legal procedures is finished. In this chapter there are seven topics.

Tassuddānaṃ (The summary verses have not been translated.)

Paṇḍulohitakā bhikkhū,
sayaṃ bhaṇḍanakārakā;
Tādise upasaṅkamma,
ussahiṃsu ca bhaṇḍane.

Anuppannāpi jāyanti,
uppannānipi vaḍḍhare;
Appicchā pesalā bhikkhū,
ujjhāyanti padassato.

Saddhammaṭṭhitiko buddho,
sayambhū aggapuggalo;
Āṇāpesi tajjanīya,
kammaṃ sāvatthiyaṃ jino.

Asammukhāppaṭipucchāp-
paṭiññāya katañca yaṃ;
Anāpatti adesane,
desitāya katañca yaṃ.

Acodetvā asāretvā,
anāropetvā ca yaṃ kataṃ;
Asammukhā adhammena,
vaggena cāpi yaṃ kataṃ.

Appaṭipucchā adhammena,
puna vaggena yaṃ kataṃ;
Appaṭiññāya adhammena,
vaggena cāpi yaṃ kataṃ.

Anāpatti adhammena,
vaggena cāpi yaṃ kataṃ;
Adesanāgāminiyā,
adhammavaggameva ca.

Desitāya adhammena,
vaggenāpi tatheva ca;
Acodetvā adhammena,
vaggenāpi tatheva ca.

Asāretvā adhammena,
vaggenāpi tatheva ca;
Anāropetvā adhammena,
vaggenāpi tatheva ca.

Kaṇhavāranayeneva,
sukkavāraṃ vijāniyā;
Saṃgho ākaṅkhamāno ca,
yassa tajjanīyaṃ kare.

Bhaṇḍanaṃ bālo saṃsaṭṭho,
adhisīle ajjhācāre;
Atidiṭṭhivipannassa,
saṃgho tajjanīyaṃ kare.

Buddhadhammassa saṃghassa,
avaṇṇaṃ yo ca bhāsati;
Tiṇṇannampi ca bhikkhūnaṃ,
saṃgho tajjaniyaṃ kare.

Bhaṇḍanaṃ kārako eko,
bālo saṃsagganissito;
Adhisīle ajjhācāre,
tatheva atidiṭṭhiyā.

Buddhadhammassa saṃghassa,
avaṇṇaṃ yo ca bhāsati;
Tajjanīyakammakato,
evaṃ sammānuvattanā.

Upasampadanissayā,
sāmaṇeraṃ upaṭṭhanā;
Ovādasammatenāpi,
na kare tajjanīkato.

Nāpajje tañca āpattiṃ,
tādisañca tato paraṃ;
Kammañca kammike cāpi,
na garahe tathāvidho.

Uposathaṃ pavāraṇaṃ,
pakatattassa naṭṭhape;
Savacaniṃ anuvādo,
okāso codanena ca.

Sāraṇaṃ sampayogañca,
na kareyya tathāvidho;
Upasampadanissayā,
sāmaṇeraṃ upaṭṭhanā.

Ovādasammatenāpi,
pañcahaṅgehi na sammati;
Tañcāpajjati āpattiṃ,
tādisañca tato paraṃ.

Kammañca kammike cāpi,
garahanto na sammati;
Uposathaṃ pavāraṇaṃ,
savacanīyā ca novādo.

Okāso codanañceva,
sāraṇā sampayojanā;
Imehaṭṭhaṅgehi yo yutto,
tajjanānupasammati.

Kaṇhavāranayeneva,
sukkavāraṃ vijāniyā;
Bālo āpattibahulo,
saṃsaṭṭhopi ca seyyaso.

Niyassakammaṃ sambuddho,
āṇāpesi mahāmuni;
Kīṭāgirismiṃ dve bhikkhū,
assajipunabbasukā.

Anācārañca vividhaṃ,
ācariṃsu asaññatā;
Pabbājanīyaṃ sambuddho,
kammaṃ sāvatthiyaṃ jino;
Macchikāsaṇḍe sudhammo,
cittassāvāsiko ahu.

Jātivādena khuṃseti,
sudhammo cittupāsakaṃ;
Paṭisāraṇīyakammaṃ,
āṇāpesi tathāgato.

Kosambiyaṃ channaṃ bhikkhuṃ,
Nicchantāpattiṃ passituṃ;
Adassane ukkhipituṃ,
Āṇāpesi jinuttamo.

Channo taṃyeva āpattiṃ,
paṭikātuṃ na icchati;
Ukkhepanāppaṭikamme,
āṇāpesi vināyako.

Pāpadiṭṭhi ariṭṭhassa,
āsi aññāṇanissitā;
Diṭṭhiyāppaṭinissagge,
ukkhepaṃ jinabhāsitaṃ.

Niyassakammaṃ pabbajjaṃ,
tatheva paṭisāraṇī;
Adassanāppaṭikamme,
anissagge ca diṭṭhiyā.

Davānācārūpaghāti,
micchāājīvameva ca;
Pabbājanīyakammamhi,
atirekapadā ime.

Alābhāvaṇṇā dve pañca,
dve pañcakāti nāmakā;
Paṭisāraṇīyakammamhi,
atirekapadā ime.

Tajjanīyaṃ niyassañca,
duve kammāpi sādisā;
Pabbajjā paṭisārī ca,
atthi padātirittatā.

Tayo ukkhepanā kammā,
sadisā te vibhattito;
Tajjanīyanayenāpi,
sesakammaṃ vijāniyāti.

Kammakkhandhako niṭṭhito. The chapter on legal procedures is finished.
